#computer science multi word dictionary extracted from Bharatvani site by Prashant. Formatted by Roja (03-10-2019)
#Changes:: 1) Separated single word and multi words into separate dictionaries
#          2) English words are converted to lower case
#          3) Added category as 'noun' by default
#          4) If last word is not punctuation then treated last word as head
#             or else treated last but one word as head
#	   5) Removed information present in  ( ) Ex:Advective thunder storm aBivahanI wadZIw JaMJA (aBivAhI wadZiw JaMJA)
			to advective_thunder_storm	aBivahanI_wadZIw_JaMJA
